PostScript names

PostScript names

Warning

Handjet Regular (Handjet[EGRD,ESHP,wght].ttf)

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Is longer:
'arLam.init_arAlifHamzabelow.fina
arLam.medi_arAlifHamzabelow.fina
arLam.init_arLam.medi_arHeh.fina
arHehGoal.init_arYehBarri.fina

arHehDoachashmi.medi_arYehBarri.fina

arYehFarsi.medi_arYehBarri.fina

arYehHamza.medi_arYehBarri.fina
_part.arTwodotshorizontalabove
_part.arTwodotshorizontalbelow'
